Domestic News

The Central Committee and National Government's Memorial Week 54

At 9:00 AM on the 10th, the Central Committee of the Party held its 85th weekly memorial service for the Premier in the grand hall of the Central Party Headquarters. Central Committee members Ma Chaojun, Zhu Jiahua, Liu Luyin, Chen Lifu, Fang Juehui, Zhang Zhen, Wang Boling, Kexinge, Yu Jingtang, Chen Yaoyuan, and others, as well as officials from various departments and commissions and guests, totaling approximately 500 people, attended. Chairman Ma Chaojun presided over the ceremony. Zhu Jiahua gave a report, stating that he had just arrived in Nanjing from Guangzhou and, based on his experience in education over the past few months, believed that intensifying educational work was a fundamental requirement for party and national construction. He then elaborated on the following points: (1) Education based on the Three Principles of the People is clearly stipulated in the party's educational policy. The party and education are inextricably linked and must be united as one. Separating them into two would be dangerous. Recently, there have been reactionary elements scheming and engaging in activities in schools, creating political obstacles. This is because they have fundamentally failed to understand the Three Principles of the People. Therefore, the responsibility must be attributed to education. The most important task in modern education is to ensure that the general public has a clear and unwavering understanding of the principles so that the principles can be realized and education can have value. (2) The center of construction lies in economics and talent, with talent being even more critical than economics. The construction guidelines issued by the Central Committee, from the province to the county, are often stalled or shelved. In some cases, workers in a county lack the knowledge of building construction and do not even know what a blueprint is. How can construction be properly carried out? This example shows that education and construction are closely related. To carry out construction, it is essential to focus on education. (3) Chinese culture has a long and brilliant history and holds an important position in the world. This is undeniable by both China and foreign countries. However, today, China lags behind in everything, and its inherent culture is on the verge of extinction. This is extremely dangerous. The lives of Chinese people are more difficult than those of any other country. While this is partly due to the social environment, the biggest reason is the low level of knowledge. To seek survival and happiness for humanity, it is necessary to use the effectiveness of education to increase their knowledge. (4) Recently, reports of internal disputes and disturbances in universities have been common, which is regrettable. Education is the mother of all things. If internal stability cannot be maintained, how can talent be cultivated and how can any cause be achieved? From the party's perspective, it is necessary to resolve these issues quickly without hesitation, lest education be fundamentally and significantly affected. (5) The rebellion of Yan and Feng caused significant sacrifices and losses for the central government and local areas. Although the suppression of the rebellion has been successful, the vitality is difficult to restore quickly. While Yan and Feng have the ambitions of warlords and do not hesitate to harm the people and the country, if intellectuals had not participated in the rebellion, their arrogance might not have been so great. It can even be said that the Yan-Feng rebellion was caused by intellectuals. It can be seen that the level of national knowledge is related to the governance and stability of the country. Therefore, fundamental construction lies in providing a solid foundation for national education. The meeting was adjourned after the report. The National Government also held a weekly memorial service for the Premier at 10:00 AM. Zhu Peide, Yang Shuzhuang, Ma Fuxiang, Jiang Menglin, Yi Peiji, Zhang Nanxian, Liu Ruiheng, Lin Xiang, Chou Ao, Wei Daoming, Chen Yi, Li Jinlun, Chen Yu, Zhou Yawei, Zhang Wohua, Wu Siyu, and over 200 officials from the National Government's civil service and military affairs departments attended. Chairman Zhu Peide presided over the ceremony, and Secretary Qian Changzhao gave a political report: "[Today, I will briefly report on three matters related to domestic and international affairs.] The Preparatory Committee for the Disarmament Conference of the League of Nations opened on the 6th, aiming to draft a disarmament agreement for discussion at the formal disarmament conference next year. The most important points of this draft agreement, which has been underway for five years, are: (1) reduction of land, sea, and air military equipment; (2) reduction of other applicable items of land, sea, and air forces; (3) restriction of military budgets of various countries; (4) prohibition of chemical weapons warfare; and (5) miscellaneous provisions. The above five points are all very proper and urgently needed. However, there may be many disputes at this conference. Relations between France and Italy have not been very good recently, especially regarding the issue of naval equality, and they do not yield to each other. Even between Britain, France, and Italy, there does not seem to be any deep understanding. Russia is putting on a high show and watching from the sidelines. Under these circumstances, it is indeed not easy to obtain a satisfactory solution. In short, some countries at the conference take facts as the premise and only consider their own interests and security; some countries use ideals as a slogan and deliberately make things difficult; and some countries, due to their status, may not be respected internationally even if they express fair views. Therefore, the atmosphere at the first meeting was tense, and the future results are still unknown. The Fourth Plenary Session will open on the 12th of this month. Now that the military suppression of the rebellion has ended, it is urgent to refresh politics, and the Fourth Plenary Session is a major key to refreshing politics. Its significance is unimaginable. The Central Committee is very confident in its overall reorganization, because the success of all undertakings depends on determination and perseverance. The Central Committee's determination to refresh politics is very clear, and we can be even more confident in our future perseverance. With determination, we can go all out and overcome all kinds of difficulties. With perseverance, we can persist to the end and reach our destination. If politics can get on the right track from now on, and the new life of the Republic of China can be promoted and nurtured from this point on, then it will be the supreme happiness of the people of the whole country. The Industrial and Commercial Conference closed last Saturday. Representatives from various ministries and commissions of the Central Committee and provincial and municipal governments, as well as leaders and experts from the industrial and commercial sectors, gathered together and repeatedly discussed and carefully decided on more than 400 proposals within eight days, which is truly rare. The resolutions of each case are of great importance to the national economy and the people's livelihood. Through this conference, the government has a clearer understanding of the real situation of the industrial and commercial sectors, and the industrial and commercial sectors have a clearer understanding of the government's sincere intention to support the industrial and commercial sectors. In the future, the government will promptly remove obstacles and actively promote and encourage. The industrial and commercial sectors will also make special efforts to cooperate sincerely with the government. In short, the conference has now closed, and there is still much work to be done. We hope and believe that by the time the second conference is held, the situation of industry and commerce across the country will have improved significantly, unlike the current situation, which is often in danger."

Zhang Xueliang's Preparations Before Entering the Pass 55

First Inspecting Military and Political Facilities in Tianjin and Hebei, with Accompanying Staff Divided into Four Departments, Communications from Shenyang: Zhang Xueliang had long prepared to enter the pass. The main reasons were: first, to inspect the military and political situation in Tianjin and Hebei to facilitate reorganization; and second, to meet with Commander-in-Chief Chiang to discuss the aftermath in the north. The reason for the delay was that representatives from various parties came one after another for consultations. Amidst these ongoing discussions with no clear direction, it was inconvenient to ignore them. Moreover, at the beginning of the troops taking over defenses in Tianjin and Hebei, thorough planning was required for the front lines and especially the rear. Meetings were held repeatedly, wasting time. Furthermore, the organization of the Deputy Commander's Office seemed to require its establishment before proceeding. Therefore, Zhang's departure date was repeatedly postponed. Currently, the following points have been resolved separately by Zhang: (1) The issue of Yan's aftermath has been telegraphed to the central government for consultation. However, a thorough solution will require a fundamental decision after meeting with Commander-in-Chief Chiang. Zhang expressed this to the representatives of the cabinet, Wen Chouquan and Liang Ruzhou, yesterday. (2) The issue of Shi's aftermath has been satisfactorily resolved. Zhang agreed to allocate 600,000 yuan in military pay each month, with the defense area set along the Pinghan Line in the Shunde area. Shi is scheduled to leave Shenyang on the 7th, passing through Tianjin and Hebei, and may stay for some time to meet with Wang Shuchang and Yu Xuezhong. (3) Regarding the organization of the Deputy Commander's Office, Zhang previously telegraphed the central government, stating that it was scheduled to be established at the beginning of this month. Currently, most preparations are complete, and the fixed number of personnel, both civil and military, totals 151, with 117 military officials and 34 civil officials. The military officials include 37 directors, deputy directors, section chiefs, chief advisers, chiefs of staff, advisers, and staff officers, all of whom are appointed to positions with the ranks of lieutenant general, major general, or colonel. There are also 51 staff officers, adjutants, section members, section chiefs, and section clerks, all of whom are delegated to positions with the ranks of lieutenant colonel or major. There are also 29 adjutants, section clerks, dispatchers, and clerks, all of whom are commissioned to positions with the ranks of captain, lieutenant, or second lieutenant. The civil officials include 10 directors, secretaries, counselors, directors, and section chiefs, all of whom are appointed to positions. There are also 8 section chiefs, section clerks, investigators, and secretaries, all of whom are delegated to positions. There are also 16 clerks, secretaries, recorders, and employees, all of whom are commissioned to positions. All of the above tasks have been clarified, and Zhang has begun to prepare for entering the pass. It is planned that, in addition to He Fenglin and Wang Shuhan accompanying him, four departments will be organized for convenience: (1) General Affairs Department: Zhu Guangmu; (2) Secretariat: Ye Biliang; (3) Staff Department: Bao Wenwei; and (4) Adjutant Department: Huang Xiansheng. The internal staff of each department has also been largely assigned to handle the affairs of the headquarters. Zhang's itinerary is decided as follows: the first step is to go to Tianjin to investigate the local military and political facilities, and the second step is to go to Beiping to inspect the stationed troops. Although there are various rumors about the location of the meeting with Commander-in-Chief Chiang, such as Tianjin, Beiping, Qingdao, or Nanjing, nothing is final. The location will be determined temporarily by Chiang and Zhang. Zhang's guards have been ordered to depart, taking the Beijing-Ningbo train to Huludao first. The cavalry unit departed on the night of the 3rd, the pistol team departed on the night of the 4th, and the infantry unit departed at 3:00 PM on the 5th, all arriving in Tianjin to await orders. Zhang's departure date is set for the 7th of this month. The Shenyang Railway Station has prepared a special train and started the fire yesterday, waiting for departure. It is reported that the two army commanders, Wang Shuchang and Yu Xuezhong, have coordinated welcome arrangements. Yu Xuezhong also ordered Han Mengxiong, the commander of the first squadron of the Northeast armored train, and Zhao Liangbi, the commander of the second squadron, to lead the team to Shenyang as the escort train for Zhang's departure (6th).

The Problem of Prohibiting the Planting of Tobacco Seedlings in Southern Fujian 56

The government ordered the stationed troops to jointly and strictly prohibit it. The Central Anti-Smoking Commission previously received a request from the Fujian Provincial Anti-Smoking Commission to forward a telegram to the National Government, instructing the troops in Fujian Province to jointly and strictly prohibit the planting of tobacco seedlings with the county governments. If tobacco seedlings are found, the stationed troops and local officials should be punished together. The case was approved by the Executive Yuan in Directive No. 2841 and forwarded to the National Government for review. The commission also instructed the Fujian Provincial Anti-Smoking Commission to take note. It is now reported that the National Government, after receiving the report, has instructed the headquarters and the troops stationed in Fujian to comply and maintain the anti-smoking policy.

Shandong Province Supplements the Levy of Head Tax and Land Tax 57

Jinan Correspondence: Wang Xiangrong, Director of the Finance Department, stated that due to the current extreme financial difficulties in the province, he recently requested and obtained approval from the provincial government to uniformly supplement the levy of the head tax and land tax for the 19th year in all counties that had not remitted it to the provincial government but had instead used it to subsidize military expenses. The subsidized funds would be allocated by the provincial treasury in installments over the years. The text of the announcement issued by the department is as follows: "[It is found that the head tax and land tax account for the majority of Shandong's annual revenue, and the entire year's expenditure relies on it. However, since the outbreak of the war, the finances have become increasingly chaotic. Various counties in southern Shandong, western Shandong, and eastern Jiaodong have either fallen into war zones or been occupied by miscellaneous troops, and Jin troops have illegally occupied Hebei for an especially long time. The majority of military expenses have been provided by the head tax and land tax. Fortunately, the war has subsided and order has gradually been restored. However, the losses in tax revenue are too great, and how can the annual budget be maintained? The Director of this department has been pondering day and night, unable to bear the distress. At this time of decline and unhealed wounds, we are unwilling to lightly discuss increasing the levy and burdening the people again, and other taxes yield little revenue, making it difficult to remedy the situation. In the absence of any other feasible method, as a way to make up for the shortfall, we are imitating the method of the former Director Yuan to supplement the levy of the head tax and land tax for the 18th year and plan to supplement the levy of the head tax and land tax for the 19th year used to subsidize military expenses, in order to provide relief and allocate the subsidized military expenses from the provincial treasury in installments over the years. This is in the nature of a loan and does not increase the burden on the people. It has been approved and implemented by the Provincial Political Conference. In addition to issuing an order to all counties to comply and open the levy within a time limit, we hereby issue an announcement to all the people of the province for their knowledge.] (December 8th)"

Shandong Will Establish a Agar-Agar Training Institute 58

Jinan Correspondence: Agar-agar, a type of food in our country, all comes from Japan, where it is called "kanten." The total value of annual imports to various parts of our country is over 600,000 yuan. Liang Daoyuan, a native of Huang County in this province, has traveled to Japan three times to join workers in learning the manufacture of agar-agar. The raw material for agar-agar is a type of seaweed, which in our country is commonly known as "cattle hair." It is abundant in the twelve coastal counties of Shandong, as well as in the eight coastal counties of Liaoning and the four coastal counties of Hebei. In the first year of the Xuantong period of the late Qing Dynasty, when someone initiated the Shandong Agar-Agar Company in Qingdao, Sun Baoqi, the Governor of Shandong, approved its establishment and raised over 45,000 yuan in shares. The company was about to begin operations, but the Wuhan Uprising affected Shandong, and the matter was suspended. Later, someone initiated the company in Yantai in the first year of the Republic of China, but it split into two places, Qingdao and Yantai, due to disagreements among the organizers, and the attempt ultimately failed. At that time, Liang Daoyuan was one of the initiators. He believed that the seaweed raw material was the same as that produced in Japan, and the output was very abundant, but it was discarded on the ground, which was a pity. Therefore, he went to Japan to study manufacturing technology in order to make a comeback. Now, Mr. Liang has returned to China after completing his studies and has a great understanding of manufacturing technology. Recently, he obtained approval from the National Government in Nanjing to establish a agar-agar training institute in Shandong. He came to Jinan to consult with the provincial government on the implementation. All the members of the provincial government expressed their strong support and believed that it could be done. According to Mr. Liang's plan, a training institute will be established first, with two trainees from each of the twelve coastal counties entering the institute for training. In the future, a general sales office will be established in Qingdao, which is scheduled to open in March next year. It is estimated that if 10,000 catties are produced, a net profit of 10,000 yuan can be obtained. According to the planned plan, it will be gradually expanded, and in the third year, 600,000 catties can be produced, yielding a profit of 600,000 yuan, which can supply the whole country and recover the rights and interests. As for the fundraising method, it is planned that each of the twelve coastal counties will subscribe for 2,000 yuan (100 yuan per share), and the Qingdao and Yantai Chambers of Commerce will each subscribe for 2,000 yuan. The provincial government will also subscribe for 2,000 yuan as promotion, raising a total of 30,000 yuan. 10,000 yuan will be used to build a factory and purchase machinery, and 20,000 yuan will be used as working capital, which will always be operated jointly by the government and merchants. If this matter succeeds, it will also be a major promising industry in the province. (November 8th)"

Airplane Crashes During Test Flight in Guangdong 59

Falling from a thousand feet in the sky, the pilot and mechanic drowned simultaneously. Guangzhou communication: The war in Guilin Province, Nanning, is still in a stalemate. The Aviation Department of the Eighth Route Army Headquarters, in order to increase its air force strength, specifically telegraphed the rear Aviation Department to allocate aircraft to the front for orders. The Aviation Department immediately prepared to send Yingde and Nanxiong aircraft to Wuzhou. Li Fengxuan, Director of the Aviation School's instructors, also volunteered to go. Mr. Li planned to practice flying before departing, so this morning (4th) at approximately 6:00 AM, he and mechanic Liu Quan piloted the German William-style No. 6 aircraft from Xiamen Aviation School for a test flight. The aircraft had two seats, one in the front and one in the back. Li, the pilot, was in the front seat driving, while mechanic Liu Quan sat in the back. Before the flight, they had prepared a sufficient amount of gasoline, intending for a long flight and to test the engine power. The test flight lasted about two hours. At 8:20 AM, the aircraft had soared into the clouds, about three thousand feet high. Mr. Li was skilled in piloting and had experience, so he was able to stay in the air for so long. Unexpectedly, when ascending into the misty clouds, the aircraft's engine was corroded by cold air, causing it to fail completely. At the same time, all the horsepower was lost, and the propeller stopped. The entire aircraft plunged towards the ground. Since the propeller could not be started, the pilot naturally could not control it and had to quickly fasten the belt around his body to the aircraft to prevent the aircraft from tilting and causing the person to fall. Therefore, as the aircraft tumbled and fell, the two men descended with the plane. About ten minutes after the accident, the aircraft had descended to about a thousand feet from the ground. Mr. Li used his skills to steer the falling aircraft towards the Dashatou airfield, hoping to accurately land in the airfield or be rescued by people in the field and be safe. At 8:30 AM, people at the airfield suddenly heard the aircraft's engine rattling in the air, different from the usual sound, and knew something was wrong. They quickly reported it to Director Huang Guangrui. Upon receiving the report, Director Huang immediately dispatched Deputy Adjutant Jian and Adjutant Yu Wenying to find a way to rescue them. Unexpectedly, in an instant, the No. 6 aircraft involved in the accident crashed into the river near the east corner of the airfield. The ships were terrified and lost color, initially not expecting the aircraft to crash. When the aircraft landed on the water surface, it unfortunately landed upside down. Li and Liu were pressed by the plane, and in the rush, they did not have time to remove the belts tied to the aircraft, causing their hands and feet to be unable to move freely. Even skilled swimmers could not escape the danger. The two men then suffocated and died in the water. It was said that if the two men had untied the belts fastened to the aircraft before going into the water, they might have been spared. When the aircraft crashed, rescuers from the Aviation Department had set out in small motorboats to salvage it from the river. At about 11:00 AM, they finally managed to hoist the No. 6 aircraft out of the water. Li and Liu's faces were gray, and officials spat blood. The death was very tragic. At that time, the two men's bodies were still firmly tied to the aircraft. The Aviation Department then untied the bodies of the two men and sent them to the Yueguang Funeral Company for preparation and notified the deceased's families to go to the funeral. At the same time, it was reported to the Eighth Route Army Headquarters for assistance in accordance with the regulations for those who died in the line of duty, and separate compensation was given. It was found that Mr. Li was from Fuzhou, Fujian Province, 38 years old. He graduated from the American Aviation School and returned to China to serve as a flying instructor at the Xiamen Aviation School. The school recently suspended operations due to funding shortages. The personnel of the school switched to the Guangdong Aviation Department. Mr. Li excelled in technology and is currently the Principal Instructor at the Guangdong Air School. Liu was 36 years old, from Panyu. He joined the Aviation Department in 1921 and was proficient in mechanics. Now, the two men have unexpectedly encountered an accident at the same time, and the talent in aviation has been weakened by two more people. (Evening of November 4th)

Communist Suspect Case Occurs in Jilin 60

The principal of the provincial No. 5 middle school was arrested, and the students were dismissed. Jilin Communication: At noon on the 30th of last month, more than 50 students from the Provincial No. 5 Middle School in Dongjuzi Street, the provincial capital, lined up and entered the city to report to Commander Xi Dai (Qia) of the Border Defense Department about communist elements within the school, requesting strict handling. Xi happened to be working at the Army Training Center at the time and immediately received them, instructing them to return to the school and wait for instructions. He immediately sent Provincial Government Secretary Zhao Rumei to lead soldiers to search the school and ordered the military police to closely monitor the situation. As a result, two large boxes of books considered to be suspected of communism were found. Xi immediately sent Secretary Zhao to Shenyang to report to Zhang Zuoxiang and ask for instructions. However, according to the school authorities, this matter was caused by six or seven unruly students who failed the exam and had to repeat the grade. These students thought that they would inevitably have to leave the school, so they spared no effort to destroy the school in every possible way. In addition, they were incited by the dismissed art teacher Zhu Yishi, so they falsely accused the school in the name of the Communist Party to vent personal grievances and destroy the school. The school has a total of more than 400 students. Except for the above-mentioned group, the rest are still attending classes as usual. Since then, the students who reported the case and the students who protected the school have issued declarations attacking each other. People generally thought that school turmoil was commonplace, and the suspicion of communism was not yet confirmed, so few people paid attention to it. Unexpectedly, on the 3rd of this month, the reported Principal Xiao Bofu and Dean of Academics Xie Yutian and a dozen other people were suddenly arrested. It is said that after Zhang Zuoxiang received Secretary Zhao's report, he believed that in the current situation of rampant communist disasters, even if there was only suspicion, the truth should be thoroughly investigated. Therefore, he telegraphed Xi to thoroughly investigate the matter. Secretary Zhao also returned to the province to report, and the authorities ordered the military police monitoring the school not to allow teachers and students in the school to move freely. The arrested people were secretly interrogated at the Border Defense Department's military court the day before yesterday and are still detained in the Public Security Bureau of the provincial capital. To this day, the authorities have not announced the content of the case. The students in the school, upon hearing the news of the arrest of the principal and others, gathered on the evening of the 3rd to discuss ways to rescue them. After the police detected this, they reported it to Xi, who telegraphed the Guard Regiment on the morning of the 4th to send a battalion of soldiers to suppress them. The military, police, and police jointly sent all the students in the school home in batches and ordered their parents to sign guarantees that they would not go out and cause trouble. Out-of-county

Page 8

boarders are still under strict surveillance by the military police and are not allowed to leave the school. As a result, the school has completely come to a standstill. The Education Department believes that the school cannot be without someone in charge, so it has appointed Dong Xianqiao, the school's director of affairs and Chinese teacher, to serve as acting principal. However, he cannot perform his duties and is only responsible for safekeeping. It is said that the authorities have criticized Education Department Director Wang Xinlin, a relative of Principal Xiao, and Wang is uneasy and has been acting passively in recent days, with talk of resigning. (November 5th)

The Secret of the Russian Consulate's New House in Harbin 61

Three-story building with a basement built with trenches. Doors and windows are equipped with iron gates, and the conference room has an underground passage.

Harbin Communication: The Russian Consulate in Harbin was originally renting a private house at No. 7 Jilin Street, Qinjiagang. After being searched by our side once on May 27 last year, the secret of its construction has been made public. In early spring this year, Consul General Melinikov requested the China Eastern Railway to allocate a new building for the consulate. His reason was that Chinese non-railway-related institutions, such as the special zone land bureau and local courts, all used official China Eastern Railway houses, and the Russian consulate should not be an exception. At that time, he also requested the allocation of the residence that Ma Zhongjun (Director of the Heilongjiang Foreign Affairs Bureau) sold to the Railway Bureau for the consulate's use. Mo Dehui did not allow it. After repeated requests, the old building of the Eastern Railway Library was allocated to the consulate. In late October, the Russian Consulate moved to the new site. However, before the relocation, the Eastern Railway Bureau actually appropriated a huge sum of one million rubles (equivalent to 2 million Shanghai taels) without the approval of the board of directors to build a new house for the Russian Consulate. The address is behind the new consulate site. Few Chinese railway employees knew about its engineering plan, and many Russian employees in the engineering department did not know the details. Construction has been underway for nearly three months, and more than half of the three-story building has been completed. The date of completion should not be far away. The highest authorities of the special zone once sent personnel to investigate the construction content of the new house. However, when they arrived at the construction site, they were refused entry by the Russian supervisor. They secretly inquired with the Chinese workers. Although there were dozens of Chinese workers, they all said that they only received wages every day or did some insignificant work outside the construction area. They were not allowed to enter the interior, and they did not know what the structure was like. After the authorities received the report, they became more suspicious, so they sent many secret agents to search for the blueprints of the house. A copy of the blueprints was obtained until recently, but it was only a partial sketch. The entire blueprints could not be obtained. However, the works recorded in this partial blueprint are enough to make people stunned, and the secrets of the entire project are far more than several times that. According to the blueprints, the building has three floors and one basement. The walls are four feet thick, and the stone foundation is fifteen feet. The windows and doors have iron gates that are five inches thick. Each window is equipped with an ordinary cannonball that cannot be destroyed. The basement windows are two feet above the ground and are separated by iron plates. The windowsill is wide enough to place a small cannon or a machine gun. There is a live gun eye inside that can see outwards. Two new-style trench-covering ditches are built inside the windowsill, which are long and surround the entire building. The top is covered with steel plates, and more than a hundred armed soldiers can be ambushed at the same time. The entrance and exit of the basement is in the Consul General's office. An underground passage from the Consul General's office can lead to the conference room. The room can accommodate 200 people. The lights and candles are installed in the walls, and the tables and chairs are not visible on weekdays. In case of emergency, the mechanism can be twisted to make them appear in rows. Behind the conference room, there is an underground passage on the wall that leads to the car room in the backyard. The car room can accommodate more than a dozen cars. The Consul General's and Deputy Consul General's offices each have a secret room, which can be used to store documents and also has criminal machinery. In addition to the obvious doors and windows, each room inside has a secret door that can be connected. In addition, there are various agencies because the original drawings are in Russian and the translated names have not been determined. Generally, they are nothing more than mechanical equipment. The new house of the Russian Consulate has this secret. Its intention is not difficult to guess. The current authorities have sent the blueprints along with the drawings to the Northeast authorities. (5th)

Local Communications

Suzhou 62

Jiangsu Province's Joint Defense Plan: The Civil Affairs Department convened a winter defense meeting on October 20, gathering water and land public security officials from various counties in Jiangsu. At that time, it was resolved that the counties in Jiangsu would be divided into joint defense zones. Zhang Zhongli, Section Chief of the Third Section of the Civil Affairs Department, has prepared a joint defense plan, dividing the province into fifteen joint defense zones. Wu County, Kunshan, Qingpu, and Wujiang are divided into the twelfth zone, with Wu County as the center. County Magistrate Huang has telegraphed the county magistrates of Kunshan, Qingpu, and Wujiang to hold a joint defense meeting in Wu County on the 14th of this month to discuss the Xiao Qinghu bandit plan during the winter defense period. Urgent Dispatch of Customs Tariff Treasury Bills: The County Government received an order from the Finance Department yesterday (10th) stating that military affairs have ended and a large amount of funds are needed, urging the dispatch of 20,000 yuan in customs tariff treasury bills to be delivered to the Jiangsu Bank nearby before the 15th. County Magistrate Huang received the order and immediately consulted with the Finance Bureau to discuss the matter. Rear Hospital to be Abolished: The Military Affairs Department sent Commissioner Song to Suzhou yesterday (10th) to meet with County Magistrate Huang at the County Government to discuss the reward money for the wounded soldiers in the 15th and 17th rear hospitals in order to comply with the order to abolish the rear hospitals. It is heard that the abolition period is not far away. Chefang Village Bandits Rob Merchant Ships: Merchant ships passing through Qixingmiao in Chefang Village were captured and robbed by lake bandits the day before yesterday. The First Chuan Branch of the Water Police went to pursue them, but the bandits had already fled. Gansu Reviews Counter-Revolution Case: Ganyu County gentleman Wang Zuoliang was accused by the people of the county to the Nanjing Special Court in 1928, saying that Wang colluded with Zhang Zongchang to provide military funds of 480,000 yuan and other counter-revolutionary acts. He was arrested and interrogated. Later, because the Special Court was abolished, Wang Zuoliang and the entire case files were transferred to the Supreme Court. Last year, the Supreme Court issued the case to the Jiangsu Higher Court for trial. In December last year, the court ruled that the evidence was insufficient and declared him innocent. At that time, the original prosecutor Jin Henian refused to accept the judgment and appealed to the Supreme Court. Wang Zuoliang submitted a written guarantee in the summer of this year and was released on bail of 11,000 yuan to await trial. Now, the Supreme Court has sent the case back to the Higher Court for retrial. Yesterday (10th) afternoon, Lin Dawen, Presiding Judge of the Criminal Division of the Higher Court, tried the case. Wang Zuoliang hired lawyer Cai Nipei to appear in court to defend him.

Wuxi 63

Business Registration to be Held Soon: The Jiangsu Provincial Government, in order to make up for the province's financial expenditures and prepare business taxes to offset the loss of tariffs, specially convened representatives of chambers of commerce from various counties in the province to hold a meeting in the province to decide to conduct business registration first. The Finance Department has drafted detailed rules for trial implementation and appointed business registration fee collection directors for various counties. Zhu Shengwu was appointed as the collection director of this county. Director Zhu came to Wuxi from the province yesterday and set up an office in the County Finance Bureau. Business registration will begin soon. All merchants in the county must go to register in accordance with the regulations and pay a registration fee of two per thousand of the capital amount. Conflict over Increased Wages in the Incense Industry: Disputes between labor and management in the incense industry in this county have been frequent. Recently, the labor side demanded a 20% increase in wages from the management side due to the increasing cost of living. The county party and government meetings repeatedly convened mediation meetings. The management side refused to increase wages due to the sharp decline in business in various stores, resulting in a breakdown in negotiations and a conflict. The labor representatives Shi Chongxun and others sent the management representative Xie Xigui to the County Public Security Bureau for legal relief. Yesterday, Bao Tiyu, a member of the Third Section, opened a court to interrogate the reasons of the labor and management sides, but he could not judge because each held its own ground. He ordered them to be sent to the county for trial. Court Record of the Liyang Old Series Fraud Case: Since the 8th, after the provincial government transferred the arrested County Magistrate Zheng Chengyuan and Finance Bureau Director Pan Bin and eleven others to the court, Chief Prosecutor Xu Shixun and Prosecutor Yan Changtao of the Local Court opened a preliminary trial that evening. They first summoned Cao Huipan, son of Cao Qingyun, recorder of the Liyang County Government (i.e., bookkeeper of the Finance Bureau), Shen Zhiqin, head of the Finance Bureau's field tax, and Huang Xing'an, head of the field tax who surrendered himself after being dismissed by Zheng Chengyuan, for investigation. At first, they were interrogated separately, and then the three were asked to confront each other. The interrogation was stern and solemn. Then, the interrogation of Pan Bin, Director of the Finance Bureau, lasted the longest. When Zheng Chengyuan was interrogated, he was eloquent and seemed to be justified. In the end, they were interrogated separately, including Ren Shuchun, Director of the Education Bureau, Di Hongxun, Director of the General Affairs Section, Shi Taorong, Director of the Organization Department of the Liyang County Party Affairs Consolidation Committee, Shi Qinglian, and Hu Jinghua, Zhou Shi, District Chief of the Fourth District of Liyang. In total, the interrogation lasted from 7:00 PM to 12:00 AM before it was completed. They were ordered to be sent to the detention center. At first, all the prisoners requested bail, but none were granted. The prisoners were treated well in custody, and there were several other county magistrates, public security directors, and trial officials who were detained for other cases, so Zheng Chengyuan and others should not worry about being lonely. Implementation of Joint Defense Plan in Various Counties: In order to fundamentally eliminate banditry in various counties, the Civil Affairs Department has specially drafted joint defense measures for various counties, regardless of provincial and county water and land boundaries, to achieve the goal of jointly encircling and suppressing bandits. In addition to Zhenjiang, Jiangdu, Danyang, Jurong, and Zhenyangzhong, which are included in the provincial guard area, the remaining counties are divided into fifteen districts. Wuxi, Wujin, Jiangyin, Changshu, and other four counties are one district. It is stipulated that a meeting will be convened in Wuxi with Pan Zhongjia, County Magistrate of Wuxi, as the director of the joint defense district. The number of police teams, public security bureaus, special police teams, and security guards in each township and town in the joint defense district, as well as the number of guns and bullets, should be investigated and properly equipped by each county and reported to the director of the joint defense district for planning. It is also stipulated that the method of distributing the teams (1) The county police team, in addition to leaving a large part to defend the key areas of the county, should draw at least one-tenth of them to be formed into guerrillas in the joint defense district and directly under the unified dispatch of the director of the joint defense district. (2) The special police team of the public security bureau of each county may draw a certain number of people to listen to the dispatch of the director of the joint defense district when necessary. (3) In addition to stationing in their own township and town, each county's security group must draw at least four-tenths of them to be formed into guerrillas, which are jointly organized by the townships and towns of Kunlian to assist the county police team in case of insufficient force. The above-mentioned measures are limited to convening a meeting one month in advance to properly discuss the implementation and submit it for approval.

Changzhou 64

Extortion Failed, Arson and Burning of Houses: Bandit forces are rampant in the fourth district of Wu County. Chen Zhangbao, a wealthy household in Dongqiangmen Village in the district, received letters of extortion and fraud from bandits one after another. He moved to the city with his family and sent people to pretend to contact the bandits. Only a few field workers lived in the house. Unexpectedly, more than 20 armed bandits suddenly came to his house the night before last, fired shots to demonstrate, and then pried open the door and searched the house. Since they found nothing, they poured kerosene all over the house and set it on fire. The bandits surrounded the house on all sides and did not allow others to put out the fire. Six houses were burned, and all agricultural tools, sundries, piglets, etc. were burned to ashes, with a loss of about two to three thousand yuan. The person involved, Chen Zhangbao, learned about it the next day and did not dare to report the case. Arrested in Cheng for Defaulting on Public Funds: Wu Huai, County Magistrate of Wu County, according to the report of the Grain Storage Committee, claimed that Miao Junru defaulted on the committee's public funds of more than 15,000 yuan and 5,000 yuan in treasury bills. It was found that Miao's address was in Shangcun Village, Shengang Township, Jiangyin. Wu County Magistrate ordered the committee member Sun Youguang to go to Cheng on the 8th and submit a document to the Public Security Bureau. Director Li ordered the police to arrest Miao Junru so that he could be sent to Changzhou for handling.

Changshu 65

New Cruiser Borrowing Quick-Firing Guns: The coast near Hupu, Fushan, Baimao, and other places in this county is easily accessible to bandits. Tan County Magistrate has approved the people's request to order a warship from Shanghai for patrol. It is now heard that the ship has been repaired and guns, sirens, etc. have been equipped. However, it is not easy to select and equip quick-firing guns for the time being. It is planned to borrow one 3.71-pound gun and one 4.73-pound gun from the Third District Department of the Water Public Security Team for application. Shen, the district chief, has submitted a report to the province for instructions. As for the issue of the captain of the ship, Yang Qingjiu, the 13th squad leader of the Water Police, and Qian Bin, the captain of the Public Security Team, will serve as the captain and deputy captain for the time being. Wang Baijin's Young Son Escapes Danger: Wang Baijin, a rice merchant who often travels between places, was suddenly robbed by bandits in the Yangtze River on his way from Chang to Tong and was seriously injured. He went to a hospital in Nantong for treatment and had his eight-year-old son (named Genda) kidnapped. It is now learned that Wang Baijin has recovered from his injuries and was discharged from the hospital. He came to Chang the day before yesterday and said that his young son Genda had also escaped danger. On the 4th of this month, the Nantong police launched a large-scale campaign to suppress bandits. When the bandits fled, the police chased them to the reeds in Da'an Port and caught sight of a boat. They knew it was a bandit boat and boarded it for a search. They only saw two boatmen. Then, they opened the deck and saw Wang Baijin's young son inside. He was rescued and taken to the bureau, and then Baijin was notified to come and claim him.

Yesterday (8th), the county interrogated them. After the interrogation, Liu Hongcai was ordered to be interrogated. The police were ordered to guard the place. Zhenjiang 67

Soldier Shot and Killed at Dashikou: At about 8:00 PM last night (9th), the Mingxing Cinema in Dashikou, Zhongshan Road, was showing a popular movie when suddenly someone came out of the cinema and had a conflict at the door. Then gunshots were heard and several police officers and bystanders ran away. Several soldiers were injured, and one soldier was seriously injured. He ran dozens of steps before falling to the ground. He was immediately taken to the Provincial Hospital for treatment. It was heard that the seriously injured person was Chen Chi, a soldier from the machine gun company of the 3rd battalion of the 11th brigade of the 6th division. The bullet went through his military cap, entered his left forehead, and exited his lower jaw. The situation was dangerous. By 9:30 PM, he was unable to speak and soon died. The other injured, Xie Zhouzong, Ma Jiagan, Xu Zongpu, and three others, were also heard to be soldiers of the 6th division. They went to the Provincial Hospital for treatment that night. Xie's left eye was injured by a bullet and the eyeball was broken. Ma's right leg was pierced by a bullet from behind. Xu's left ear was stabbed by a knife. He was slightly injured and did not stay in the hospital. In addition, Zhu Shizhong, a policeman from the mounted patrol team of the Provincial Public Security Bureau, was shot in his left arm, and the bullet passed through the upper part of his anterior pelvis. It was heard that after treatment by the hospital, none of them were in danger. Cart Driver Fights Porter: At Xiaomatou, the small railway crossing, at about 1:00 PM yesterday (9th), cart drivers Ji Dekui and Shen Shaochuan and porters Zhai Zhengyang and Cao Jia'an had a conflict over business. The two sides fought fiercely with each other. The cart driver used a knife and the porter used a stick. At that time, more and more people gathered, and both sides were seriously injured. The 7th branch sent police to bring the cart driver's accomplices Gao Chengyou, Yuan Jinhong, Tang Weihe, Gao Yihui, Long Xixian, and five others, as well as the seriously injured Hua Jianzhi, to the bureau. Officer Zheng believed that a bloody case had occurred and that Zhai Zhengyang, Hua Jianzhi, Liu Dianliang, and others were seriously injured, so he immediately transferred them to the court for handling.

Jiaxing 68

As a result of the failed mediation, the Public Security Bureau sent the case to the Jiaxing Local Branch Court for review.

Door-to-Door Rice Prices Soar: Since Xin Jian's appearance, rice prices in Jiaxing have been low and have fallen to 10 yuan and 2 jiao. People in the middle class are happy. Unexpectedly, the Rice Price Review Council decided to increase the price of rice to 10 yuan and 9 jiao yesterday and the day before yesterday. The prices of various rice stalls have increased by 4 jiao and 6 jiao. According to the reason for the soaring prices, the goods are scarce, and merchants come to purchase rice, resulting in insufficient supply and prices have to increase. According to insiders, this situation will continue to rise and increase in the future.

Sea Bandits Engage in a Real Firefight

The Sanjia town sea bandit Pan Kaiwu is now engaged in a real firefight with the sea bandits Shen Guanxi and Shen Guanshou due to disagreements. They were successively submitted to the provincial government for review and approval. Now, upon receiving a telegram stating that Guo Xi'er and the other twelve people, as well as Xu Wenyuan, have all confessed to their crimes and are approved to be executed by firing squad. As for Miao Sheng, in addition to being suspected of counter-revolutionary activities, there is no interrogation confirming his bandit behavior, and he should be transferred to the Jiangsu Higher Court for trial. Robbery of a Ship Suspected to Be a Misunderstanding

A widowed daughter-in-law surnamed Yuan was kidnapped. The bandits learned of this and within only two hours of her arrival, eight bandits suddenly came and kidnapped her to Hangzhou.

The Silk Industry Suddenly Declines

The sales of the Hangzhou silk industry gradually increased after the end of the military operations, and the price of goods also increased. However, recently, it has suddenly declined. The reason for this is that the end of the national calendar year is approaching, and the deadline for settlement is imminent. All the farms did not dare to indiscriminately collect goods, and the same situation exists for the customer gangs. Sales are consequently sluggish. Strictly Prohibit Disturbing the People in the Name of Enlistment

Yesterday, the Provincial Bandit Suppression Headquarters issued a notice to all subordinate areas strictly prohibiting the practice of disturbing the people in the name of enlistment. If any such cases are discovered again, they should be immediately arrested to ensure local stability. It is difficult to stop the collection of religious donation taxes. Those in Zhejiang Province who collect religious donation taxes to fund education have used them for construction and public welfare expenses. This time, the Ministry of the Interior requested that the collection be stopped. The Provincial Government believes that this donation tax has been in place for a long time, and chanting scriptures and worshiping are the responsibilities of wealthy families. Taking it from the people and using it for the people is difficult to stop. Yesterday, a special request was submitted to the Executive Yuan, enumerating the various reasons why the abolition of local funds would inevitably lead to budgetary deficits and affect the undertaking of public works. Please postpone the suspension of the educational message.

Important News: Heilongjiang Province Plans to Establish More Secondary Schools 72

Six Education Development Plans are Formulated to Establish Fifteen Middle Schools Within Five Years

Harbin Dispatch: The Heilongjiang Provincial Government is seeking to develop the current state of education in the province and has stipulated a plan to increase the number of middle schools in each county. The first step is to add eleven junior middle schools for boys and four junior middle schools for girls within five years. Among them, in addition to the restoration of the First Girls' Middle School in the provincial capital, the other counties where schools will be established are as follows: (1) One boys' middle school and one girls' middle school will be established in Hailar. (2) One boys' middle school will be established in Nehe. (3) One boys' middle school and one girls' middle school will be established in Deli. (4) One boys' middle school will be established in Tangyuan. (5) One boys' middle school will be established in Zhaozhou. (6) One boys' middle school will be established in Baiquan. (7) One boys' middle school will be established in Tuiyi. (8) One boys' middle school will be established in Manzhouli. (9) One boys' middle school will be established in Mohe. (10) One boys' middle school will be established in Wuyun. (11) One boys' middle school will be established in Solun. (12) One girls' middle school will be established in Suihua. If county middle schools have already been established in the above-mentioned areas, they will be expanded and transformed into provincial schools based on their original foundation. All original funds of the county middle schools will be transferred to the province to offset the insufficient amount, which will be borne by the provincial treasury. The second step is to continue adding primary and secondary schools in Shizhang, Qigan, Huma, Kete, Luobei, and Suidong year by year within five to ten years to popularize education.

Yesterday 74

Yu Youren Goes to Zhonggong, Mr. Yu's Sincere and Touching Admonishment, Conflict Between the Delegation and the League (National News Agency)

Yu Youren, the new president of China Public School, arrived at the school to inspect the situation yesterday (the 10th) at 3 p.m. Posters with slogans such as "Welcome Party-State Elder Yu, the President," "Welcome Central Committee Member Yu, the President," "Welcome the Founder of Our School, Yu, the President," "Welcome President Yu to Purge Reactionary Elements," "Down with the Communist Party," "Down with the Statist Faction," "Down with the Reorganization Faction," "Long Live the Chinese Kuomintang," and "Long Live China Public School" were pasted all over the school. When Mr. Yu's car arrived near the Paotaiwan Station, the welcoming delegation set off firecrackers to welcome him. The entire student body gathered at the large playground, and Mr. Yu immediately took the stage to deliver an admonishment, which stated roughly: I have come to the school today to maintain school affairs, not to assume office. I am here at the repeated urging of the school affairs council and the students, and seeing that the school has fallen into a state of anarchy and the students' studies have been completely suspended, I could not bear it, so I came to the school to maintain order. You should abide by the resolutions of the board of directors. Before the board of directors appoints another successor, I will be fully responsible. If you have any opinions, you can send one or two representatives to speak, but the number of people should not be too large, and there is no need to organize a delegation. Mr. Ma has resigned. The board of directors has not resolved to ask him to return to the school, and he will not come back. In short, all matters must be resolved by the board of directors. Now, you must concentrate on your studies and not act like children. Supporting someone and overthrowing someone is all nonsense. I will soon have to go to Beijing to attend the Fourth Plenary Session of the Central Committee. You must not act rashly, etc. There was thunderous applause throughout the speech.

Another News Item

Since President Ma Junwu of China Public School in Wusong resigned and went to Japan, and Yu Youren was elected as president, the students have been divided into two factions: one is the delegation, and the other is the League. Yesterday morning, the delegation side, because the board of directors had elected Yu Youren as the president of Zhonggong, and Mr. Yu was scheduled to come to the school at 2 p.m. on the 10th to take office, the students held an emergency meeting to strike first to show their rejection and issued various slogans such as vowing to support President Ma's return to the school. At the same time, the League side also posted various slogans on top of the delegation's slogans, causing a conflict between the two factions. Yang Fanrong, the chief of the 7th District, learned of this and immediately supervised Inspector Dai Guosheng and Yulong, along with eight police officers, to rush to suppress the situation. At 3 p.m., Mr. Yu, wearing a gray silk robe and carrying a cane, arrived at the school by car. When Mr. Yu had just entered the school gate, a large number of students from the delegation side shouted to support President Ma, and some people shouted to overthrow Secretary Ding Guyin, causing the order to be extremely chaotic and indescribable. Later, after Mr. Yu rested for a while, he stood high in the school's gateball field and declared to the public that he had not come to take over as president, nor had he ever been president, and that he wanted to go to Beijing to attend the Fourth Plenary Session of the Central Committee, so he had no time to be president. He had come to Songjiang on the entrustment of President Cai of the board of directors and Hu Shih to temporarily maintain order, etc. He also advised the students to abide by the school rules and to prioritize their studies so as not to waste their precious time. After speaking, he got into the car and returned to Shanghai. It is heard that Ma Junwu will probably arrive in Shanghai today. It is also learned that Yu Youren, at the repeated urging of the board of directors, faculty, and students of China Public School, went to the school at 3 p.m. yesterday to announce his intention to temporarily maintain order. When Mr. Yu's car passed Jiangwan, a small number of people held a meeting inside the school to disrupt the school, and military police were requested to maintain order. He immediately sent someone to order the military police to withdraw, otherwise, he would not go to the school. After the military police withdrew, the students welcomed Mr. Yu into the president's office to handle affairs. Because there were too many listeners, the auditorium was not big enough, so the meeting was changed to an open-air meeting in the sports field. Mr. Yu's speech mainly covered: (1) The board of directors elected me as president this time, but I am sick and have too many things to do, so I have repeatedly declined. (2) The chairman of the board of directors repeatedly urged me, because the school is in a state of disorder, and the various problems are getting bigger and more complicated, and because Mr. Cai and I are going to Beijing to attend the Fourth Plenary Session of the Central Committee, the board of directors cannot convene the school and no one is responsible, fearing that it will delay the students' studies. I had no choice but to come to the school today to maintain order, but I am not here to take office, but to temporarily maintain order. (3) The various major problems in the school will be resolved by the board of directors. Students should serve the board of directors' resolutions and should start attending classes as usual. (4) I still hope that the board of directors will elect someone else. Mr. Hu Shih advised me to wait for Mr. Ma Junwu to return to the school together before taking office. I am not here to take office, so why wait for Mr. Ma? Before Mr. Yu took the stage, a small number of restless students hoped to disrupt the meeting, but when Mr. Yu spoke, the whole audience was convinced and dispersed with cheers.

Municipal Education Bureau Assesses School Principals' Performance 77

Drafts Measures for Evaluating the Performance of Principals of Municipal Primary and Secondary Schools

The Municipal Education Bureau has recently drafted temporary measures for evaluating the performance of principals of municipal primary and secondary schools in order to assess their performance. The measures have been submitted to the Municipal Government and the Ministry of Education for approval and filing. The text of the articles is extracted as follows: Temporary Measures for Evaluating the Performance of Principals of Municipal Primary and Secondary Schools in Shanghai

1. The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau has formulated these measures to assess the performance of principals of municipal primary and secondary schools in order to encourage improvement.

2. Principals of municipal primary and secondary schools who meet the following requirements may be commended by the Bureau in various ways:

(1) Able to diligently implement the Three People's Principles of education.

(2) Possessing sound character and serving as a role model for the entire school.

(3) Focusing on their duties and making significant progress in improving school affairs.

(4) Determining teaching implementation methods and allocating subject time appropriately.

(5) Appointing teachers and staff who are qualified and dedicated to school affairs.

(6) Students achieving excellent results and verified by the Bureau.

(7) Having an appropriate administrative organization system and implementing it accordingly.

(8) Managing school finances openly, allocating them appropriately, and reporting them legally.

(9) Handling school affairs in accordance with current laws and regulations.

(10) Completing tasks assigned by the competent authority on schedule and properly.

3. The commendations for principals of municipal primary and secondary schools are divided into the following categories:

(1) Recording a commendation.

(2) Awarding a certificate or prize.

(3) Increasing salary grade.

(4) Extending the term of appointment or employment.

(5) Other.

4. If a principal of a municipal secondary school violates any of the matters listed in Article 4 of the Shanghai Municipal Secondary School Principals' Appointment and Dismissal Rules, and the Bureau verifies the violation, they shall be punished accordingly.

5. If a principal of a municipal primary school violates any of the matters listed in Article 5 of the Shanghai Municipal Primary School Principals' Appointment and Dismissal Rules, and the Bureau verifies the violation, they shall be punished accordingly.

6. The punishments for principals of municipal primary and secondary schools are divided into the following categories:

(1) Issuing a reprimand.

(2) Revoking a certificate or prize.

(3) Decreasing salary grade.

(4) Suspending their duties at the end of the semester.

(5) Temporarily suspending their duties.

7. The rewards and punishments for principals of municipal primary and secondary schools shall be decided by a review committee consisting of three to five members recommended by the Bureau Affairs Meeting, based on the inspectors' reports and other documents. The review committee shall deliberate and decide on the matters and issue a written opinion to the Bureau Affairs Meeting for joint decision.

8. The rewards and punishments for principals of municipal primary and secondary schools shall be executed by the Bureau Director. Major rewards and punishments must be submitted to the Municipal Government for approval and implementation.

9. These measures shall be implemented from the date of approval by the Municipal Government.

Joint Research Association for Elementary Teaching 81

Dong Renjian Speaks on How to Use Textbooks

The Joint Research Association for Elementary Teaching in this city held its thirteenth regular meeting at He'an Primary School on the 8th. More than sixty people from sixteen schools, including Wuben Attached Primary School, First Experimental Primary School, Shangzhong Experimental Primary School, Wanzhu, Xicheng, and He'an, attended. They first visited the work of elementary children at He'an School for the exhibition room and equipment. The meeting was held at 2:00 p.m., with Qian Xuanqing presiding and Chen Shuying recording the minutes. After the chairman's report, Mr. Dong Renjian was invited to speak on how to use textbooks. He said that to study this problem, we must first understand the advantages and disadvantages of using textbooks. Regarding the advantages: (1) Using textbooks makes teaching easy to learn. (2) Textbooks have a well-organized curriculum. (3) Using textbooks makes each level more complete. Regarding the disadvantages: (1) It cannot take into account the different abilities of children in the whole grade and has no flexibility. (2) The teaching materials often do not conform to the differences in children's personalities, local differences, and differences of the times. (3) Editors often have prejudices. (4) Due to psychological effects, it is not easy to find errors in textbooks. (5) Textbooks include too little. (6) It is easy to mistakenly regard textbooks as the gospel, which shackles thought and makes it difficult to be independent. If so, how should we use textbooks? (1) First, we must understand the book, such as the publishing house, the name of the editor, the publication date, whether it has been reviewed, and the table of contents, etc. must be recognized first. (2) Pay attention to the children's learning process, first arouse the motivation to read, then let them read quickly, but not carefully, then read slowly, and then practice repeatedly. (3) Use the textbook as a method to initiate discussion and solve problems. (4) Use the textbook as a guide for work. (5) Use the textbook as a supplementary reading material. Then, he explained in detail how to use reference books, etc. After the speech, there was a discussion. (A) A discussion on how to deal with the report of examples of elementary national arithmetic teaching received. As a result, those already received will be mimeographed by the original school and distributed to each school for reference. Those not received will continue to be collected and processed at the next regular meeting. (B) A discussion on how to formulate a perfect elementary children's self-government organization and implementation methods to increase educational efficiency. Shangzhong Experimental Primary School supplemented the reasons and methods. As a result, first collect materials (including children's lives and the good habits they need), organize them, and then distribute them to each school for reference, and nominate Shangzhong Experimental Primary School to preside over and other schools to assist in collecting materials. (C) A discussion on how to guide low-grade children to read. As a result, Longde First Experimental Primary School was nominated and other schools assisted in collecting materials (refer to Mr. Dong Renjian's speech). (D) A discussion on the school on duty for the next regular meeting. Yucai Primary School was nominated. The discussion adjourned at 6:00 p.m.

Local News

Chairman Chiang and Wife Passed Through Shanghai Yesterday on Their Way Back to Beijing 94

Naval Guns Fired, Security Along the Way Was Tight

Received Yu Youren, Li Shizeng, Sun Hongyi, and Others in the Afternoon

Chairman Chiang of the National Government, accompanied by his wife, Madam Soong Mei-ling, arrived in Shanghai yesterday afternoon from Ningbo aboard the Lianjing warship, and took the 11 PM night train back to Beijing that evening. He met with Vice Commander Zhang, received French Ambassador Wilden, and attended the Fourth Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee. A detailed account of yesterday's events in Shanghai is provided below:

Kong Xiangxi Accompanied Chairman Chiang and his wife departed from their ancestral home in Fenghua at 6:30 PM on the 9th, arriving in Ningbo at 8:50 PM. They then boarded the Lianjing warship, dispatched by the Navy, and sailed to Shanghai. Those accompanying them included Kong Xiangxi and his wife and children, Wang Shihe, the chief of security, and Jiang Fushou, the adjutant, totaling more than ten people. Secretary Gao Lingbai had already gone to Beijing earlier. Zhu Peide had already returned to Shanghai.

Yongjian Warship Did Not Arrive According to Wang Shihe's statement to this newspaper's reporter yesterday, the Yongjian warship was originally responsible for escorting the Lianjing, sailing ahead. However, when it arrived at Zhenhai, its rudder tail was suddenly damaged and it had to return for repairs. There was a slight wind and waves in the evening, which reduced the speed of the Lianjing. Chairman Chiang originally intended to arrive in Wusong at 5:00 or 6:00 AM, stay in Shanghai, and then proceed to Nanjing. Unexpectedly, it did not arrive until 12:00 noon, so the plan was changed.

A Seven-Hour Wait Shanghai-Wusong Garrison Commander Xiong Shihui received a message the night before that Chairman Chiang would land at Gaochangmiao. Yesterday morning around 5:00 AM, he dispatched a team of detectives from the command headquarters to guard the Gaochangmiao naval dock. Xiong himself also rushed to welcome him at 6:00 AM, but waited until 9:00 AM without seeing any sign of him. Finally, he was informed by the Wusong garrison that everyone had moved to Wusong to welcome him. Cars from both the Chiang and Kong residences had driven to Wusong at 4:00 AM yesterday morning to welcome them. Various key members of the Navy Department also arrived at the Wusong dock around 5:00 AM. The Lianjing warship did not arrive until 12:00 noon. The welcoming party waited for seven hours.

Tight Security After 9:00 AM yesterday morning, there was still no news of the Lianjing warship arriving in Song, but more and more people who had heard the news came to welcome him. These included Xiong Shihui, Yuan Liang, Chen Xunyong, the commander of the naval training fleet, Wu Zhennan, the head of the coastal defense, Jiang Bin, the commander of the Wusong fortress, and dozens of reporters from various newspapers. Near the Wusong naval dock, the Second Battalion of the 27th Regiment of the 5th Division stationed in Song was responsible for security and defense. The entire vehicle patrol team of the Public Security Bureau and armed police officers from the command headquarters assisted, making the situation quite serious.

Twenty-One Gun Salute It wasn't until after 11:00 AM yesterday morning that the white smoke of the Lianjing warship was seen. At 11:45 AM, the ship arrived at the mouth of Wusong. Navy Vice Minister Chen Shaokuan happened to be returning to Shanghai aboard the Chuyou warship after a maneuver. The Lianjing warship stopped slightly outside the mouth of the river. Chen went aboard to pay his respects, and the Chuyou warship fired a 21-gun salute to express its welcome. At 12:15 PM, the Lianjing warship arrived at the naval dock. Chiang and others boarded small gasoline-powered boats to come ashore. At 12:30 PM, they landed. The entire Lianjing warship was painted white and fully decorated with national flags. When Chairman Chiang and his wife disembarked from the small boat, the Lianjing warship also fired a 21-gun salute in tribute. The sound of cannons echoed loudly, shaking the eardrums.

Received Yu Youren After landing, Chairman Chiang and his wife took separate cars to the Kong residence for lunch. They then went to a private residence on Gallier Road to rest. Yang Hu, Wu Zhihao, and others came to pay their respects, but they were not received. Around 4:00 PM, Chairman Chiang and his wife went to get their teeth done on Great Britain Road, and then visited the tomb of Madam Soong's father in the International Cemetery on Hongqiao Road. At 5:30 PM, they returned to the Soong residence on Seymour Road. They then summoned Yu Youren, Li Shizeng, and Sun Hongyi to discuss important official matters. In the evening, they attended a banquet hosted by Kong Xiangxi and his wife, with Huang Jinrong, Du Yuesheng, Zhang Xiaolin, and others as guests. At 9:30 PM, they went out for a drive. At 10:45 PM, they arrived at the North Station.

Took a Special Train to Beijing Last night at 11:00 PM, Chairman Chiang and his wife took a special train to Beijing. The area around the station was secured in advance by a company of soldiers from the 27th Regiment, dispatched by the Shanghai-Wusong Garrison Command. The Public Security Bureau also dispatched armed police and soldiers from the 48th Division to assist in maintaining order. Those who went to the station to see them off included Kong Xiangxi and his wife, Xiong Shihui, Chu Qiaqing, Chen Xizeng, Zhou Peizhen, Song Ziliang, and others. Chiang Yi, the deputy director of the command headquarters, and the head of the detective team also arrived at the station to direct operations. Chairman Chiang and his wife rode in a PCA&T Pullman car. When Chiang and others arrived at the station, the Public Security Bureau's military band played music to welcome them. After Chiang boarded the train, he took off his hat on the train and thanked the welcoming party.

Wang Zhengtin and Others Traveled Together Chairman Chiang's train was a special train, leaving fifteen minutes before the overnight express train. There were a total of four Pullman cars and four sleeping cars on the train. In addition to the Pullman car occupied by Chairman Chiang and his wife, those traveling to Beijing on the same train included Foreign Minister Wang Zhengting in Pullman car No. 14, Zhejiang Provincial Government Chairman Zhang Jingjiang in Pullman car No. 12, and Guangdong Provincial Government Chairman Chen Mingshu in Pullman car No. 2. Li Shizeng, Dai Jitao, Chen Ce, Wang Jiazhen, Zheng Hongnian, and Zhang Shouchong were in the sleeping cars.

Vice Commander Arriving in Beijing According to Vice Minister Wang Jiazhen, Vice Commander Zhang is expected to arrive in Beijing at 11:00 AM tomorrow (the 11th). Therefore, Chairman Chiang and others hurriedly left Shanghai last night to go to Beijing to welcome Vice Commander Zhang. Vice Commander Zhang will stay in Beijing for a short time and then return to Peiping and Tianjin to handle the aftermath of the North, and may not have time to visit Shanghai.
